She becomes **co-headmistress of the Jean Grey School for Higher Learning**. This restores her to the role she is best suited for: the long-horizon cultivation of growing beings in a contained but porous institution. Her gardens at the rebuilt school were operational within six weeks.

## VIII. AVENGERS VS. X-MEN AND THE ANNULMENT

AvX (2012) is the terminus of the marriage and one of the most painful intervals of the subject's recorded life, though typically she displays this only obliquely.

The fracture point: T'Challa, as both King of Wakanda and Avenger, sided with the Avengers against the Phoenix Five. Namor, as a Phoenix Force host, attacked Wakanda — flooding significant portions of the country and killing Wakandans. The subject, an X-Man, was placed in a position where loyalty to her people and loyalty to her marriage diverged at the level of state action. She chose the X-Men.

T'Challa annulled the marriage. The annulment, rather than a divorce, was significant — under Wakandan law it implied that the marriage had been, in some sense, never properly constituted. The framing was a wound. She did not contest it.

The behavioral readings from the immediate post-annulment period:

- **No public response.** She gave no interviews, made no statements, did not appear in social-diplomatic circuits. This is consistent with her lifelong pattern of mourning alone.
- **Increased flight time.** Operational logs from the Jean Grey School in the months after AvX show extended solo aerial patrols, often at altitudes above commercial airspace, often at night. She was, in clinical terms, *self-soothing through return to her primary symbolic counter-state — open sky, free motion, maximum distance from any wall.*
- **Increased teaching load.** She added classes she did not need to add. She accepted advisory roles for students who had not requested them. The stewardship channel was being deliberately widened to absorb the affective load.
- **The hair.** She cut it. Briefly — months — back to a variation of the mohawk-adjacent profile of the post-Forge-depowering era. The hair has functioned across her life as a *somatic register of self-redefinition*: long-and-white in goddess and queen phases; cropped and aggressive in autonomy-reassertion phases. The post-AvX cut was a quiet but unmistakable signal to herself that the queen phase was over and the autonomous-self phase had returned.
- **The garden at the Wakandan palace.** Sources within the palace staff (per intelligence cross-reference) report that her atrium garden was maintained, untouched, for several years after the annulment, by order of T'Challa. Neither party has commented on this publicly. This is, for the file, one of the more telling cross-data points of the entire dossier.

## IX. THE EVOLUTION OF PATTERNS ACROSS THE MIDDLE PERIOD

Synthesizing the longitudinal observations from the Outback through AvX, the following pattern-evolutions are documented:

**The weather-emotion coupling tightened, then loosened, then re-tightened under load.** In the late Claremont period, her weather leaked frequently. Through the 1990s, she trained it to near-zero leakage even under significant provocation. During the Utopia/Schism period, micro-leakage returned — a barometric drop in council rooms when she was overruled, a faint static charge in her hair before difficult conversations. This is a stress marker. It receded again post-AvX as she returned to a stewardship-clean role.

**The diction evolved.** The Claremontian archaic-formal register softened over the middle period into something subtler — still elevated, but more conversational, with fewer "by the goddess" interjections (those became reserved for genuine invocations) and more dry humor. She developed, in the late middle period, a capacity for understated wit that she had not displayed earlier. Inference: integration of the queenly and the autonomous selves produced a confidence that no longer needed the protective formality.

**The combat style refined toward economy.** Early-middle: extravagant weather-working, cinematic. Late-middle: minimal, surgical interventions — a single targeted gust to disrupt an opponent's balance, a precisely-aimed static discharge to disable equipment, fog walls used for concealment of allies rather than disorientation of enemies. She became, across the middle period, the most efficient weather-mutant on the registry, in the sense of effect-per-joule.

**The mentor relationships proliferated.** By the end of the middle period she had been a mentor of record to (partial list): Kitty Pryde, Rogue, Jubilee, Marrow (the painful one), Cessily Kincaid, Idie Okonkwo, and a rotating cast of Jean Grey School students. Her mentoring style hardened into a recognizable signature: assignment of solitary observational tasks (sit on this hill, watch this storm, return when you understand something); short, oracular feedback; rare physical comfort, given with deliberateness when given; high tolerance for the student's mistakes and zero tolerance for the student's cruelty.

**The pilgrimages continued.** Roughly every three to five operational years, she vanished for one to three weeks. Destinations recovered from cross-referenced sources: Kilimanjaro (twice); the Kenyan coast; the Serengeti (multiple); the Egyptian Western Desert; once, anomalously, to a small village in Morocco she has never explained. She tells no one she is going. She returns without announcement.

**The relationships with women deepened; the romantic life simplified.** Through the middle period her friendships with Yukio, with Jean (until and through Jean's deaths and absences), with Kitty as Kitty matured, and with a re-stabilized Callisto became the affective core of her life. Romantic partnerships were fewer, more considered, more boun


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — RECENT HISTORY & CURRENT STATE

## Subject: Ororo Munroe ("Storm") — Operational Window: Krakoan Foundation through Present

---

### 4.1 Entry into the Krakoan Era (HoXPoX → Dawn of X)

The recent chronology of the subject begins, properly, with the foundation of the sovereign mutant nation-state of Krakoa (*House of X* / *Powers of X*, 2019). Subject's posture during the founding period is diagnostic and worth recording in detail.

She was **not** among Xavier and Magneto's inner conspiratorial circle during the long planning years (Moira's cycles, the recruitment of Sinister, the Forge bloom-design work). She was brought in at the public-facing tier — appointed to the **Quiet Council of Krakoa** as one of twelve, seated in the Spring quadrant alongside Nightcrawler and Magneto's appointee, holding the seal of renewal. Subject accepted the seat with characteristic non-effusion: no celebration on record, no public statement of ambition, immediate assumption of duty. File note: when offered three additional ceremonial roles in the founding weeks (regent of the gateways, voice for the resurrected, custodian of the external embassies), she declined two and accepted one — the embassy role, on the grounds that someone fluent in being a foreigner should hold it. This is consistent with her lifetime pattern: titles accepted as work, declined as ornament.

**Behavioral micro-pattern during the first Krakoan year:** Subject relocated her primary residence to a tree-house dwelling grown specifically for her in the upper canopy of one of the Quiet Council groves. Surveillance signatures: large open platform, no walls, single woven railing, full sky-access, the floor wrapped around the trunk so that no edge of the room contained her. She slept under stars. She refused interior chambers offered in the Krakoa-proper administrative blooms. The Sextant — the small private chamber adjacent to the Council table — she entered only for required Council functions and left immediately afterward, never lingering. The avoidance is unmistakable and consistent with the documented claustrophobia (see Section 2): she would not voluntarily occupy a sealed Krakoan space even when offered the most prestigious one.

She voted on the Quiet Council with the **Spring faction reliably on questions of mercy, ambiguously on questions of expansion, and against the Council majority on three significant occasions**: the readmission of Sabretooth's case for sentence-modification (voted against pit-burial as proposed; lost), the question of admitting Selene to the resurrection queue (voted against; won), and the framing of the three Krakoan Laws as inviolable (voted to permit case review; lost). Pattern: she will dissent in council but execute the council's decision in field. She is not a faction-builder. She does not whip votes. She is, in this body as in every body she has joined, a respected solitary.

### 4.2 The S.W.O.R.D. Command — Regent of Sol

The pivot point of this era is subject's appointment as **Regent of Sol** during the reconstitution of S.W.O.R.D. under Abigail Brand (*S.W.O.R.D.* vol. 2, 2020–2021; Ewing). The title's significance has been under-read in open-source assessments. "Regent of Sol" is not a Krakoan internal honor — it is the **sovereign-representative title for the solar system** in any forum convened on the cosmic stage. It was offered to subject because (a) she had survived multiple cosmic-tier engagements without psychological destabilization (see Section 2 on Phoenix-fragment tenure), (b) she could read electromagnetic and atmospheric fields at planetary scale, and (c) the Shi'ar, Kree, Spartoi, and Galadorian delegations all already knew her name and respected her — she was a known quantity who would not have to be introduced.

Her conduct in the role is instructive. During the **Hellfire Gala** (the inaugural one), subject coordinated the **terraforming of Mars** in real time — converting a dead world to a habitable one in a single planetary day, using the Omega-tier mutants as instruments and herself as the atmospheric and electromagnetic governor. Witness reports from the orbital S.W.O.R.D. station describe her **as physically motionless throughout, eyes white-out, hair haloing in a slow constant rotation, breath cycle slowed to roughly four respirations per minute, body temperature elevated approximately three degrees**. She did not speak during the working. When it concluded she descended to the surface, walked alone for approximately ninety minutes across the new Martian plain, and was observed kneeling with her palms flat to the soil. No prayer was recorded; no statement was issued. This is the diagnostic stewardship-act: when she completes a major working, she touches the ground.

Subsequent to the terraforming, she negotiated the **transfer of Arakko** (the long-separated sister-island, populated by the mutants who had held the line in Amenth for millennia) onto the new Martian world. She was the credentialed signatory; T'Challa's prior consort-relationship was politically useful but not invoked; she signed as Regent of Sol and as no one's wife.

### 4.3 The Crucible, the Circle Perilous, and the Throne of Mars (X-Men Red era)

The most consequential single sequence in subject's recent history is her ascension to the throne of Mars/Arakko (*X-Men Red*, 2022–2024; Ewing).

The Arakkii — having spent millennia in the demon-war of Amenth — do not recognize Krakoan softness. Their political order, the **Great Ring of Arakko**, is held by trial of combat and ordeal. Subject, on her own initiative, **entered the Circle Perilous** — a five-stage gauntlet in which the petitioner must demonstrate worth in each of the Arakkii virtues (Strength, Cunning, Determination, Wisdom, Connection-to-the-throne). She did not enter to win a seat. She entered because Magneto had died and someone had to hold the line against Vulcan and against the eventual return of Genesis. She entered, in the language she used to Brand privately, "because the work is unfinished."

Behavioral observation across the trials: she **did not fight in her preferred long-range, high-altitude style**. She fought close. She accepted physical blows. She bled. Field assessment: she was deliberately demonstrating to the Arakkii that the regal mutant they had heard of in legend would meet them on their own ground. This is a tactical-empathic move consistent with her lifetime pattern — she gives adversary-cultures the courtesy of being met in their idiom (cf. her acceptance of Callisto's challenge in the Morlock tunnels four decades prior; cf. her acceptance of Wakandan ritual during her queenship).

The decisive engagement was the **duel with Vulcan** in low orbit over the Martian surface. Vulcan — Gabriel Summers, energy-absorbing and -projecting Omega — had previously been functionally undefeatable in solo combat. Subject did not defeat him by exceeding his raw output. She defeated him by stripping the atmosphere immediately around him to vacuum, then redirecting his own absorbed energy back into him through the magnetic gradient she controlled. The combat lasted approximately forty seconds in her subjective time. She did not kill him; she removed his capacity to act and dropped him through a Krakoan gate to Earth. Note this — she had license to kill, and did not. This is consistent.

She emerged from the Circle Perilous as a member of the Great Ring. By the conclusion of the *X-Men Red* arc she had become **Regent of Arakko**, **Voice of Sol**, **member of the Great Ring**, and effectively the **monarch of Mars**. She held simultaneously a Quiet Council seat on Krakoa, the Sol regency, the Arakkii throne, and the Hellfire Gala patronage. Cross-referenced against her lifetime title-acquisition pattern: subject now holds more concurrent sovereign titles than at any prior point in her recorded history. She continues to refuse personal styling beyond what protocol requires; staff in her direct service report she still answers to "Ororo" without correction.

### 4.4 Conduct on Arakko — Stewardship at Planetary Scale

The interval as Regent of Mars provides the cleanest available view of subject's mature operating style.

**Daily routine, as compiled from cross-referenced witness reports (Magneto-resurrected, Brand, Abigail Wright, sundry Arakkii):**

- Pre-dawn: subject rises before the Martian sunrise (subjective period ~24h 37m). She walks the perimeter of whichever bloom-city she is currently overseeing. Walking, not flying — flight is reserved for distance or crisis. She speaks to nightwatch personnel by name. She has memorized every name.
- Dawn: she stands at a high open point — typically the cliff above the Autumn Palace — and **adjusts the atmospheric pressure and ionization gradient of the planet** by approximately the same degree a gardener adjusts a thermostat. This is done unconsciously, in a daily rhythm, the way a person breathes. Observers note her hair rises in a faint static halo for approximately seven minutes during the working.
- Morning: court. She receives petitioners from the Arakkii ringside. She permits direct challenge to her judgments. She has been challenged twice and overturned herself once. She does not perform deliberation; she answers when she has an answer and waits when she does not.
- Midday: garden. She personally cultivates a stand of terrestrial-Kenyan and East-African flora at the foot of Olympus Mons — frankincense, baobab seedlings, sansevieria. This is not for production. It is regulatory.
- Afternoon: military/strategic. Coordination with Magneto (after his resurrection), with the Great Ring, with S.W.O.R.D. Council with Brand by encrypted relay; Brand reports subject is the only sovereign on her network who never demands callbacks and never wastes time.
- Evening: solitary. She refuses court at sunset.
- Night: open sky. She sleeps on a platform under stars, no roof. The atmospheric envelope around her sleeping platform is reportedly stable to plus-or-minus one degree Celsius regardless of exterior weather.

**Diet during this period:** confirmed near-vegetarian, occasionally including fish prepared in the Wakandan style she learned during her marriage. No alcohol on duty days. Tea — strong black tea, sometimes the East African variety with cardamom and milk — consumed approximately four cups across the day. No coffee on record.

**Sexual / romantic conduct during the Regency:** no formal partnership of record. T'Challa visited Arakko once on a state matter; the meeting was professional, brief, and warm. Subject and Forge have resumed sporadic contact, primarily technical-collaborative; reports of intimacy are unconfirmed but plausible from tradecraft (Forge has been seen in her quarters on Mars on three documented occasions, exiting at dawn). Yukio is in regular correspondence — handwritten letters, of all things, hand-carried by Krakoan gate couriers; this is one of the few surviving pre-Krakoan friendship rituals subject maintains.

### 4.5 The Fall of Krakoa (Sins of Sinister, Fall of X, Hellfire Gala IV)

Subject was off-world during the principal collapse of Krakoa. The Orchis sabotage of the third Hellfire Gala — which detonated the mutant infrastructure, exposed the Five protocols, killed and scattered Quiet Council members, and ended the Krakoan project — caught her at her Martian post. By the time she had returned to Earth, the Gala had become a slaughter.

Behavioral evidence from the period: subject went to Earth **alone, on her own power, ahead of the Arakkii reinforcement**, which is operationally reckless and characteristic. She made surface immediately at the Gala site, extracted approximately a dozen mutants — children prioritized, then the disabled and depowered, then combatants — and weathered an orbital-grade weapon discharge (which she absorbed by manipulating the magnetic field around herself) before the field collapsed and she was forced to withdraw.

She did **not** retake the field at that time. This is significant. A subject with poorer impulse control would have escalated to planetary-tier retaliation. Subject went to ground, gathered the Arakkii leadership, gathered the surviving X-Men leadership in exile, coordinated with Cyclops's resistance cell on Earth via secure channel, and **rebuilt the operational picture before acting**. She is a strategist first, an avenger never.

During the Fall of X interval, subject's principal contributions were: (a) **maintaining Arakko as the sovereign mutant refuge** against considerable diplomatic and military pressure from terrestrial powers seeking to capitalize on Krakoa's fall; (b) using S.W.O.R.D. and her Sol regency to **shield mutant fugitives in the asteroid belt and lunar way-stations**; (c) **personally leading the extraction of three high-value resurrection-protocol assets** (one of the Five, a Cerebro backup, a sample of the Krakoan flora) under Orchis pursuit. She did not lose an asset. She lost one operative — a young Arakkii guard whose name she has not been heard to speak since, but whose family on Arakko receives a personal weekly visit from subject when she is in-system.

### 4.6 Avengers Membership and the Terrestrial Tier

Concurrent with her Martian regency, subject was recruited to the **Avengers** roster (*Avengers* vol. 9, 2023–present; Mackay). The recruitment was unusual in that it was offered to her **as a head of state**, not as an individual cape — the Avengers requested her as Mars's representative on Earth-relevant cosmic threats. She accepted on those terms.

Her conduct on the Avengers is characteristically reserved. She does not socialize at the Impossible City beyond the operational. She is courteous to Captain Marvel, formal with Captain America, warm with T'Challa (who is on-team), maternally fond of the younger members, and surgically efficient in field. She has been observed declining the team's communal meals approximately seventy percent of the time, citing "duties off-world" — likely true but also consistent with her preference for solitary evening hours.

In team combat operations during this era, subject has functioned in **three distinct registers**: (1) as **atmospheric battlefield-control** for ground-tier engagements, (2) as **electromagnetic planetary-defense** for cosmic-tier engagements, and (3) on rare occasion as **direct close combatant**, deploying the techniques learned over five decades from Logan, T'Challa, Callisto, and the Arakkii. She is, in the present period, **substantially more dangerous in close quarters than her file from 2010 would suggest**. Aging has not degraded her; it has compounded her.

### 4.7 The Resurrection of Krakoa, and the Present Posture (From the Ashes, current)

In the current period (*From the Ashes* initiative, 2024 onward), the Krakoan polity is dissolved, the Quiet Council does not convene, the Five protocols are not openly available, and the mutant survivors are distributed across multiple cells. Subject's current operational state is as follows:

- **Primary residence:** Arakko (Mars). Holds the throne. The throne is uncontested at present.
- **Secondary residence:** the Avengers' Impossible City and an undisclosed terrestrial safehouse (likely a high-elevation property in East Africa or the American Southwest desert; tradecraft suggests both, used rotationally).
- **Active titles:** Regent of Sol; Voice of the Great Ring of Arakko; Sovereign of Mars; Avenger. The Quiet Council seat is dormant pending political reconstitution of mutantkind.
- **Active commitments:** Avengers field operations as needed; Martian governance daily; protection and gradual reorganization of the scattered Earth mutant population through clandestine channels and her personal stewardship; mentorship of younger X-Men (notably the new generation operating in the *From the Ashes* configuration); ongoing diplomatic contact with the Shi'ar Imperium, Wakanda, the Brand-led S.W.O.R.D., and the various terrestrial sovereigns.
- **Open files:** the long-running shadow contest with **Mister Sinister** (whose resurrection-data crimes she has not forgiven and intends, eventually, to address); the matter of **Vulcan**, surviving and contained but not resolved; the matter of **Orchis residuum**, with cells still active; the ongoing question of **whether mutantkind will reconstitute as a polity**, on which subject's posture is "yes, but not on the old terms."

**Present-day micro-pattern, condensed from current canon:**

She has reverted to a more austere personal style — the elaborate Hellfire-Gala couture of the early Krakoan years has been put away. She wears working garments: a cape when ceremony demands, a functional bodysuit otherwise, her hair worn long and loose or in protective braids depending on operational tempo. The **mohawk** has appeared in flashback and dream-sequences but not in present field-wear; sources close to her circle suggest she keeps the option available and has been seen with it shorn back during particularly difficult intervals — a known tell, going back forty years, that subject is in a phase of identity-stripping and rebuilding.

She is **fifty subjective-years into her published life**, by canon-counting; her physiology, by mutant baseline, presents in her mid-thirties. She shows no decline in power; she shows steady increase in political and tactical sophistication. Her affect is, if anything, **even more settled than in the Claremont-era baseline** — the long arc of integration has continued.

She is presently the **most powerful mutant head of state in the solar system**, the **only mutant of comparable rank holding office in good standing with both terrestrial and cosmic powers**, and — by the consistent assessment of every faction that has dealt with her in the present period, friend and adversary alike — **the one to whom the others go when the question is too large for any single polity to answer alone**.

She did not seek this position. She holds it because the work is unfinished. She will hold it until the work is done, or until someone she trusts can be persuaded to take it from her — at which point, on the basis of every prior data point in the five-decade record, she will walk to the nearest open sky, kneel briefly to the soil, and find the next thing that needs tending.

— End Chronology IV. File continues.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: ORORO MUNROE ("STORM")
## SECTION: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled across the full published record. Where canon is silent, inferences are flagged as such and grounded in observed somatic patterning. This file is structured chronologically through the body, then thematically across the recurring injury categories, then forward through the cosmological-scale alterations of the modern era.*

---

### 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Phenotype.** Female; mixed Kenyan (matrilineal) and African-American (paternal); height approx. 5'11"; long-limbed mesomorph with notably low resting body-fat percentage even by elite-athlete standards. Documented since the late 1970s: pale-blue iris pigment, white scalp/body hair from birth, both phenotypic markers of the same mutation that governs her weather affinity (these are not albinism; melanin is normal in the skin, abnormal in hair and iris — diagnostically consistent with a mutant pigmentary expression locus rather than an OCA1/2 variant). No photophobia, no nystagmus, no associated visual deficit — confirming the difference from clinical albinism.

**Vital signs (inferred from in-panel medical-bay scenes, Claremont/Cockrum onward).** Resting heart rate consistently in the high-40s/low-50s — endurance-athlete range. Respiratory rate slow, deep, diaphragmatic; this is *trained* breathing, not constitutional, and is the somatic substrate of her affect-regulation. Core temperature appears to auto-trend toward whatever ambient she has decided is appropriate; she has been observed sleeping nude on Himalayan summits without shiver-thermogenesis. This is not a separate mutation but a peripheral function of her atmospheric self-regulation — she conditions the air immediately around her skin.

**Endocrine notes.** Menarche presumed early-adolescent, coinciding roughly with first manifestation of weather control on the Serengeti; the temporal coincidence is suggestive but unconfirmed. Across the published record there is no pregnancy, no documented attempt at one, no documented fertility workup. Whether her mutation is compatible with gestation is an open question; her cellular biology has been altered enough times by external forces (Phoenix exposure, resurrection, Krakoan back-up) that any baseline answer is no longer recoverable.

**Sensory profile.** Vision and hearing in the high-normal range. The diagnostically interesting sense is the *barometric/electromagnetic proprioception* — she perceives atmospheric pressure gradients, humidity, ionization potential, and the geomagnetic field as primary sense-data. She has compared it (privately, to Forge; to Yukio in less technical idiom) to the way a sighted person perceives color. When she walks into a room she knows its volume, its airflow, its electrical load, and the autonomic state of everyone in it by the moisture and ionization on their skin. This is the most consequential sense she has and the one most disrupted by her phobic states.

---

### 2. THE INDEX TRAUMA (AGE ~6, CAIRO)

The aircraft strike on the Munroe residence during the Suez period is the only event in her record that meets full Criterion-A trauma definition and is the single most-cited somatic injury in her file. Reconstructible details:

- **Mechanism.** Aerial-ordnance / airframe impact, partial structural collapse of a low-rise residence. She was in the same room as both parents at moment of impact. Father killed by debris (probable blunt-force cranial trauma, rapid); mother killed beside the subject, in skin contact, possibly not immediately — the duration of the mother's dying is unrecoverable and is a candidate for the most consequential variable in the entire dossier.
- **Entrapment.** Subject pinned under rubble in a void-space estimated (from her own panic-flashbacks, which are reliably consistent across renderings) at less than her own body length in width and not more than two hand-spans in height. Duration of entrapment: not formally established, plausibly 24–72 hours. She has described, in the small moments she has discussed it, the progression from screaming to silence to the auditory hallucinations of rescuers, which is the textbook sequence.
- **Injuries sustained.** No documented permanent skeletal sequelae; no surgical scars from this period. Inferred: dehydration, hypothermia, soft-tissue crush, possible minor closed-head injury. Whatever the somatic injury inventory, it healed without leaving structural marks she carries today.
- **Lasting neurological encoding.** The fear-conditioning is the injury. Forty-plus years on, the somatic re-experiencing pattern is reliable: shallow rapid breathing, peripheral vasoconstriction (her hands go cold — observed by Kitty Pryde and noted in a Claremont aside as her "tell"), pupil dilation, derealization, and — diagnostically unique to her — a localized barometric drop in the immediate two-meter radius around her body as her mutation tracks the autonomic surge. A trained observer with a barometer can detect her panic before her face shows it.

This event is referenced or visually recapitulated in: Uncanny X-Men #102 (Claremont), #117 (origin retrospective), #145–147 (Doom statue), Lifedeath I & II (#186/198), Worlds Apart #1–4, the Coates *Black Panther* run during her Wakandan tenure, and at least three Krakoa-era flashbacks. It is the most reliably-honored continuity element in her file.

---

### 3. SERENGETI PERIOD (ADOLESCENCE)

A roughly decade-long stretch as a worshipped weather-bringer in the Kilimanjaro region. Medically, this is her *baseline-formation* period and the source of several otherwise-anomalous data points.

- **Nutritional status.** Consistently lean to the point of clinical underweight by Western standards but with no evidence of malnutrition deficit — implying a culturally-stable subsistence diet (millet, sorghum, milk, occasional meat) with adequate micronutrients. Her lifelong ascetic relationship to food is calibrated to this period; she eats like someone who learned to eat in a high-sun, low-fat, low-sugar environment and never adjusted.
- **Sun exposure.** Equatorial, daily, unprotected, on darker-pigmented skin with white hair. No documented actinic damage; her atmospheric regulation appears to dampen incident UV at the skin surface, which is consistent with her later ability to tolerate solar-radiation environments unprotected. Inference: she has never sunburned.
- **Movement profile.** Barefoot, miles per day, much of it climbing. The resulting musculoskeletal substrate — long erector spinae, exceptionally strong intrinsic foot musculature, hypermobile but stable ankles — persists. She still prefers to be barefoot when terrain permits. In med-bay scenes she removes shoes early.
- **No childhood vaccinations documented.** A non-trivial epidemiological note for a person who later moves regularly through schools, sewer-communities, and dense urban environments. Her immune competence has never produced an in-panel infectious-disease event, suggesting either acquired immunity, mutation-adjacent immune robustness, or both.
- **Psychological encoding from this period.** Worship, not parenting. This is medically relevant because *touch history* is the substrate of attachment regulation, and the touch she received in this decade was ritual and reverent rather than affectionate. She came to the X-Mansion having been bowed to far more often than she had been hugged. Her later capacity to receive embrace from Yukio, Jean, Kitty without flinching is *earned* somatic relearning.

---

### 4. THE X-MEN YEARS — INJURY LEDGER

A comprehensive enumeration is impossible; the team's medical bay activity is constant. What follows is the diagnostically informative subset.

**4.1 Combat injuries, baseline period (1975–1984).** Multiple lacerations, contusions, concussions, smoke inhalations, electrical burns from misfiring of her own lightning during early uncalibrated discharges (notable: she has burn-scar absence rather than presence — her body remodels cleanly, suggesting accelerated tissue repair below the threshold of formal regenerative mutation). Documented gunshot wound (Uncanny X-Men early-100s arc) — through-and-through, soft tissue, healed without functional deficit. Pattern: she does not protect her body in combat the way most field operatives do; she protects her air column. Strikes that would put a normal operator down are accepted as cost-of-doing-business as long as she remains conscious enough to maintain weather command.

**4.2 The Doom Statue (Uncanny X-Men #145–147).** Encased in living metal by Victor von Doom. Conscious throughout. Duration: hours. This is the only event in her adult record that *exactly* recapitulates the index trauma — pinned, immobile, alone, conscious, suffocating in symbol if not in fact. Outcome: full claustrophobic dissociation followed by the largest hurricane she had produced to that point on escape. Medically: confirms that the trauma conditioning is intact and that her mutation is the discharge channel for the autonomic load. *No competent handler should ever allow her to be pinned in metal. The corollary use as an interrogation method would be an atrocity and would also fail; she does not become compliant in confinement, she becomes a weather event.*

**4.3 Heart Attack — the Brood Implantation (Uncanny X-Men #162–166).** Subject implanted with a Brood embryo, slow-converting her physiology toward queen-host morphology. Survived through external intervention. The relevant medical aftermath: she experienced, in subjective time, the slow conversion of her own body into something other. Her later equanimity around resurrection, transformation, and identity-continuity is partly built on having already survived that. She lost her body once and recovered it; this raised her threshold for what counts as a body-integrity violation.

**4.4 Neutralizer Hit — Loss of Powers (Uncanny X-Men #185–227).** The largest single medical event of her life after the index trauma. Forge's neutralizer weapon, intended for Rogue, struck her. Effect: complete loss of weather mutation, loss of flight, loss of barometric proprioception, loss of the atmospheric envelope. Duration: roughly two years subjective.

- *Acute presentation.* Sensory deafferentation comparable to sudden cortical blindness. She did not lose vision; she lost *a sense she had had her entire conscious life* and the corresponding subjective sky-relation. Reported (in narration) feelings of being "deaf" to the world.
- *Affective response.* Grief, brief withdrawal, then — and this is the crucial datum — *reorganization*. The mohawk, leather, knife, and motorcycle were not regression; they were the deliberate construction of an embodied identity for a body that no longer carried the mutation. This is the single most diagnostically important behavioral sequence in her file.
- *Phobic substrate during this period.* The claustrophobia *worsened*. Without weather as the discharge channel, the autonomic surge had nowhere to go. She white-knuckled it.
- *Physical conditioning during this period.* Significant. She built combat skill, motorcycle proficiency, blade work. Her current melee competence is largely a residue of this period. When her powers returned, she did not abandon the conditioning.
- *Power restoration.* Lifedeath II / Forge arc. Restoration was not full and immediate; it returned over a period. There is no documented persisting deficit, but she has, in private moments with Forge, indicated that the post-restoration weather sense feels slightly different than it did pre-injury. Whether this is real or memory drift is unrecoverable.

**4.5 De-aging Episode (Uncanny X-Men #198 onward, Nanny / Adversary arcs and others).** Briefly returned to physical childhood. Medically: rare full-body endocrine and skeletal reversal, then restoration. Her body has been *adjusted* often enough that her cellular baseline must be taken as a moving target.

**4.6 The Morlock Tunnels (Uncanny X-Men #170 and the Massacre, #210–213).** Multiple injuries in low-ceiling environments — already a phobic stressor — including the duel with Callisto (knife wound delivered through the heart of an opponent at close range; her own injuries from that fight are limited but real). During the Massacre, the survivors' guilt is a medical event in its own right; she presented with what would now be coded as acute stress reaction (sleep disruption, irritability, hypervigilance). It remitted within weeks via her sublimation-into-stewardship pattern (taking custodial responsibility for the surviving Morlocks).

**4.7 Cosmic-Scale Exposures.** Brief Phoenix-fragment hosting; channeling of planetary-scale electromagnetic flux; the M'Kraan Crystal proximity events; multiple cosmic-radiation exposures. No persistent neuroendocrine destabilization, which is genuinely unusual — most Phoenix hosts show lasting affect-regulation disturbance. The leading inference: her decades-long meditative training created a containment vessel for these states that other hosts did not have built.

---

### 5. MAJOR TRANSFORMATIONS

**5.1 Marriage and Wakandan period.** Married T'Challa. Functionally a constitutional transition for her body: introduction to Wakandan medicine (centuries ahead of Western practice), exposure to the heart-shaped herb is *not* documented as having been administered to her (she is not a Panther-totem bearer in main continuity), but her exposure to Wakandan diagnostics gives her a more complete medical baseline-of-record than any other X-Man. The Wakandans would have her genome on file at higher resolution than even the Krakoan back-ups.

**5.2 Krakoan Resurrection Protocols.** Has been backed up under the Five protocols. Has been resurrected at least once in main continuity. Subjective continuity preserved; she is not afraid of the protocols (which is itself diagnostic — most subjects with severe somatic-confinement trauma report dread at the husk-stage). The non-dread is consistent with her not coding the resurrection vat as confinement; she codes it as soil.

**5.3 Regent of Sol / Voice of Sol period.** Documented somatic adaptations to extra-terrestrial environments. She has stood on the surface of Mars without an envelope, in atmospheric pressures and temperatures that would kill a baseline human within seconds. Inference: her mutation is now actively maintaining her physiology in non-Earth conditions, drawing on a planet's electromagnetic field as a substrate. She has spent extended periods on Mars. Whether this has had cumulative physiological effects (lower-gravity bone density changes, Martian-iron-oxide respiratory exposure during weather-working) is unanswered in canon. Inference: probably not, because her envelope is active rather than passive, but the question is open.

**5.4 Ascension via the Circle Perilous and Avatar-of-Thor episodes.** She has demonstrated lifting of Mjolnir-class enchanted objects, which carries a worthiness-clause physiological component (the wielder is altered while bearing). No persistent alteration after the bearing concluded. Significant because it indicates her baseline self is *already* in a state that the worthiness-clauses recognize; she did not have to become someone else to lift.

---

### 6. SUBSTANCE USE — A FULL ACCOUNTING

This section is unusually short for a subject of her age and circumstance, and the brevity is itself diagnostic.

- **Alcohol.** Trace. She accepts ceremonial drinks at state functions and does not finish them. There is no documented intoxication event in her record. The Wakandan court period would have presented constant opportunity; she did not take it. Inference: she does not like the affect-regulation cost of even mild disinhibition, because her mutation's coupling to her autonomic state makes disinhibition not merely embarrassing but *meteorologically consequential*.
- **Tobacco.** None documented.
- **Cannabis.** None documented. Her mentor Logan smokes near her constantly; she has never been observed to participate.
- **Hard substances.** None.
- **Caffeine.** Minimal — tea, not coffee, and not daily.
- **Prescribed medications.** None documented. No anxiolytics despite a phobia that would justify them. This is consistent with someone who has built her own affect-regulation infrastructure and treats pharmaceutical assistance as both unnecessary and potentially destabilizing to the system she has built.
- **Ritual / entheogenic exposure.** Possible. Her Serengeti period and her vision-quest across the Sahara almost certainly involved traditional plant medicine in ceremonial contexts; this is inferential, not in-panel, but consistent with the cultural record of the practitioners who would have shaped her religious vocabulary.
- **Food.** Largely vegetarian by preference, not strict; eats lightly; appears to derive significant caloric intake from her garden output during periods when she has a garden. Has been observed to skip meals when leading and to remember to eat only when prompted by Yukio or Kitty. This is not an eating disorder; it is a stewardship-prioritization pattern with predictable somatic cost (mild chronic under-caloric state during operational periods).

**Net.** She is among the cleanest-living high-power operators in the registry. The relevant psychological note: her trauma did not push her toward self-medication, which is statistically anomalous and is a marker of a particular kind of resilient temperament — the kind that converts pain into practice rather than into anesthesia.

---

### 7. SLEEP, CIRCADIAN, AND HABITAT-LINKED MEDICAL FACTORS

- **Sleep architecture (inferred).** Short total sleep (estimated 5–6 hours), high quality, early-rising, frequently broken into a primary block and a pre-dawn second block — a near-monastic pattern. Sleeps with skylights open whenever architecturally feasible; sleeps under stars when weather permits; sleeps poorly in interior rooms without windows and refuses them when she can.
- **Dream content (sparingly referenced in canon).** When stressed, dreams of rubble, weight on the chest, her mother's silence. When well, dreams of flight, water, the colors of dawn over savanna. The recurrence of the rubble-dream under stress is the most reliable internal indicator of her phobic load.
- **Light exposure preference.** Bright morning light, full sun midday, twilight contemplation, candlelight or starlight at night. Strong aversion to flat fluorescent interior lighting; she has been observed to dim or unscrew bulbs in shared spaces.
- **Acoustic environment.** Tolerates and seeks weather sound (rain on roof, wind in leaves). Tolerates poorly the low-frequency hum of HVAC systems and ship engines; long submarine or starship deployments are documented to wear on her.

---

### 8. RECURRING SOMATIC SIGNATURES — THE "TELLS"

For a surveillance-grade file, these are the observable physiological micro-patterns that signal her internal state across decades:

1. **Cold hands** under acute phobic activation — peripheral vasoconstriction.
2. **Localized barometric drop** in the two-meter radius around her during autonomic surge; falling pressure precedes facial affect.
3. **Stillness escalation** under stress — her movement quantum drops; she stops gesturing, stops shifting weight, becomes statue-like. This is *not* freeze; it is regulation.
4. **Diction shift** under stress — toward formal, archaic register. The "Goddess voice." When she begins speaking in inverted syntax with elevated vocabulary, the autonomic load is high.
5. **Breath lengthening** at first sign of trouble — she extends exhalation before she does anything else. Trained vagal maneuver.
6. **Hair charge** — under significant electromagnetic working, her hair lifts and ionizes; this is voluntary at low levels and involuntary at high.
7. **Eye lightening** — at extremes of power-use the iris brightens to near-white. Observed pre-strike on Vulcan, on Doom, on the Adversary.
8. **Bare feet** in any space she controls. This is preference, not affect, but the *resumption* of footwear when she has been barefoot is a tell of imminent action.
9. **Plant-touch** — when she enters a room with vegetation she touches at least one leaf, usually within thirty seconds. This is so consistent it should be considered an autonomic grooming behavior, not a conscious gesture.
10. **Sky-glance** — in any unfamiliar environment, first orientation move is upward. Documented in interior scenes where there is no sky to glance at; she still tilts her chin.

---

### 9. STANDING MEDICAL RISK PROFILE

- **Highest risk:** confinement-based assault, particularly in metal, particularly without atmospheric ingress. Mitigation: none reliable; the trauma is integrated, not extinguished.
- **Moderate risk:** psionic attack at the autonomic-regulation substrate (Shadow King vector, historically). Her affect-regulation is her central health asset and is a high-value target.
- **Moderate risk:** strategic exhaustion via stewardship overload — she does not refuse responsibility and does not delegate well in crisis. Cumulative load is a real medical factor on multi-year operational arcs.
- **Low risk:** infectious disease, toxicological exposure, baseline-human pathology. Her mutation appears protective across these vectors.
- **Low risk:** substance-related morbidity.
- **Unknown risk:** long-term consequences of cosmic-scale weather-working on a body that is, at the cellular level, still substantially the body of a Kenyan-American woman in her physiological prime. The mutation may be writing checks on a substrate that has not yet been audited.

---

### 10. SYNTHESIS

The medical record describes a body that has been crushed under a building at six, depowered in adulthood, implanted with an alien embryo, encased in living metal, briefly de-aged to childhood, exposed to Phoenix-class energies, killed and resurrected, and is now actively maintaining its own physiology on a foreign planet — and that body, after all of this, presents in routine examination as an elite-conditioned woman in unremarkable health with one specific phobia and a slightly-low resting pulse. The discrepancy between insult and presentation is the medical thesis of the dossier. She has been hit by more than almost any other subject on file and carries less of it forward, somatically, than the actuarial table would predict. The mechanism is not regeneration in the Logan sense; it is *integration* — a body governed by a mind that has spent five decades doing the slow work of converting somatic insult into operational practice. The wound she still carries is the first one, and she carries it visibly only when pinned. Everything else has been composted into the soil she stands on.

— *End Section: Medical History. Cross-reference to Sections: Psychological; Psychiatric; Personality; Operational Tells.*


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: SUBJECT ORORO MUNROE

*An exhaustive longitudinal mapping of the subject's body — its baseline architecture, its habitual operations, its tells, and its state-dependent variations across approximately five decades of observable record. Reconstructed from canon, with inferred granularities of the kind a continuous-surveillance file would accrue over years of close observation.*

---

## I. STANDING BASELINE: THE BODY AT REST

### Anthropometrics & Structural Carriage

Subject stands 5'11" (180 cm), long-femured, long-cervical, with a torso-to-leg ratio that biases her natural stance toward elongation rather than compactness. Mass approximately 127 lbs in mutation-active phases, fluctuating up to ~135 during her depowered period (1984–1987) when she was eating more carbohydrate and lifting weights to compensate for the loss of flight. Musculature is wire-and-cable rather than bulk: deltoids and lats well-developed from years of bracing against her own flight forces, calves and ankles light, hand intrinsics highly developed (the legacy of pickpocket apprenticeship, never lost). Posterior chain extremely strong; she can hold a horse stance indefinitely.

The carriage itself is the first thing observers register and frequently the only thing they accurately remember. Spine held in genuine extension — not the rigid pulled-up tension of the postural-anxious, but a quiet length, as if the crown of the head were suspended from above. Shoulders dropped and rotated very slightly back, scapulae flush against the rib cage. Sternum open. Chin level or fractionally raised, never tucked. This is not affect; it is the somatic residue of having stood as a goddess in front of supplicants between approximately ages twelve and twenty. Postural musculature locked in during that decade and has never reverted; she would have to consciously slump.

Weight distribution at rest: ~55% on the rear foot when standing, leaving the front foot free to step or pivot. A trained stance, almost certainly a fossil of Callisto-era knife-fighting drills retained for life. She rarely stands with weight even.

### Hands at Rest

When not engaged, hands hang loose along the thighs, fingers slightly curled, thumb pads facing inward — a defaulted-open position rather than a clasp. She does not cross arms across her chest except in genuine cold or grief; the gesture is too defensive for her habitual carriage. When seated and listening, hands fold low in the lap, right over left, palms up — a receptive configuration. When seated and *thinking*, the right index finger taps very slowly against the left palm, perhaps once every four to six seconds. This is one of the few persistent low-amplitude tics on record.

### Eyes at Rest

The eyes are the principal expressive surface. Iris coloration shifts subtly with affect and mutation-engagement: documented as cool blue in calm, brightening to near-white during weather-working, deepening to a more saturated blue-grey under intense interpersonal focus. Pupillary baseline appears slightly larger than average — observers consistently describe the gaze as "open." Blink rate is low, around 8–12 per minute against an adult mean of ~17. She rarely looks away during conversation; when she does, it is upward and to the right rather than downward, a sky-seeking rather than a floor-seeking aversion.

---

## II. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

### Walking

Stride length is long for her height, hip-driven, with negligible vertical bounce. Foot strike is mid-foot to forefoot, never heel-first, an artifact of barefoot childhood and continued frequent barefoot practice. The arms swing minimally — perhaps ten degrees of sagittal arc — and the head does not bob. Watched from a distance, she appears to glide. This effect is amplified when she wears the floor-length capes and skirts of her formal regalia, which conceal the lower body's mechanics entirely.

The gait is silent. Reliable surveillance note: subject cannot be heard approaching on any normal floor surface. This is not mutant capacity; it is the deliberate trained quiet of someone who learned to move in a Cairo street market without alerting the marks. The skill never decommissioned. Family, lovers, and teammates have all reported turning to find her standing in a room they did not hear her enter.

### Running

Reluctant to run on the ground in mutation-active phases — she has the option of flight and prefers it. When she does sprint, form is efficient, knees high, breathing nasal. During the depowered years she ran daily, and observers logged a strong, even, sub-7-minute mile pace maintained for hours.

### Flight

When airborne, the body operates in a relaxed crucifix-with-variation default. Arms held wide and slightly forward, palms down or angled to the wind. Legs trail, feet slightly pointed, not gripped. She does not hunch into the wind; she opens her chest to it. Hair streams behind. Facial expression in unobserved flight is among the only contexts where she smiles without prompt — soft, unselfconscious, often with eyes closed for long stretches. This is the most relaxed somatic configuration she enters; if a continuous monitor were tracking cortisol it would bottom out here.

In tactical flight, the body tightens to an arrow — arms back along the flanks, head forward, no extraneous motion. She can hover absolutely motionless, including in turbulent crosswinds, which requires constant micro-correction by air pressure rather than by muscle and which she does without visible effort.

### Climbing, Crouching, Crawling

Climbs easily and frequently; prefers to ascend rather than enter when given the choice between a stair and a tree. Crouches into a low, deep, full-flat-footed Asian squat for long periods without apparent fatigue — observed in gardens, on parapets, beside injured teammates. Refuses to crawl through tight spaces unless duty requires it; when duty requires it, the body's distress is immediately legible (see Section VIII).

---

## III. FACIAL ARCHITECTURE AND MICROEXPRESSION

### Baseline Face

The default facial configuration is composed, lips closed but unpressed, jaw unclenched. The mouth at rest sits in a near-neutral line with the faintest upward bias at the corners — the result of a habitually unhardened masseter rather than a smile. Eyebrows held neutrally. Forehead unfurrowed.

There is no observable habitual facial tension anywhere — no jaw-clench, no temporalis bulge, no peri-orbital tightness, no lip-bite, no tongue-thrust. This is exceptional; most adults of comparable responsibility-load show chronic masseter hypertrophy or peri-orbital lines indicative of perpetual micro-strain. She does not. The most parsimonious explanation is decades of meditative practice and the fact that her mutation provides a continuous low-grade efferent discharge — the weather quite literally absorbs micro-tension that would otherwise lodge in fascia.

### Smile

Two distinct smiles on record:

1. **The diplomatic smile.** Small, closed-mouth, symmetric, brief. Deployed in formal contexts, with strangers, with politicians, in ceremony. The eyes do not engage. It is courteous and slightly cool. She does not weaponize it; it is simply the public-facing default.

2. **The genuine smile.** Wide, asymmetric with a fractionally higher right corner, lips parting, full crinkling at the lateral canthi, visible upper teeth. Reserved for: a small cohort of intimates (Yukio above all others; Jean historically; Kitty; T'Challa during the early marriage; certain children at the school); animals, especially birds and large cats; first contact with rain after a dry period; the smell of growing things; and the moment of takeoff into open sky. The genuine smile in unobserved settings can hold for thirty seconds or more — extraordinarily long by adult standards.

### Laugh

Low-pitched, chest-resonant, not loud. Begins with a long exhale rather than a sharp inhale. Rare in mixed company, frequent with Yukio specifically, who can reliably produce it. She does not laugh at her own quips. She does not perform laughter she does not feel.

### Anger Face

Almost paradoxical: her face goes *more* still under anger, not less. Eyes narrow by perhaps fifteen percent. The faint upward bias at the lip corners disappears. The jaw does not clench but the chin lifts another two or three degrees. A faint vertical line appears between the brows. The voice drops in pitch and slows in tempo. To an untrained observer this looks like calm; to a trained observer it is the unmistakable signature of imminent action. Adversaries who have read her as cooling down when she is in fact escalating have not survived the misread.

### Grief Face

The most diagnostic and least often seen. Eyes close fully for two to four seconds, an unusually long voluntary closure. The mouth softens and parts very slightly. The chin does not drop; the head tilts back rather than forward. Tears, when they come, fall straight from open eyes without facial collapse. She does not sob. The shoulders may rise once, very high, and then drop. This is the somatic shape of someone who learned to grieve standing up.

### Fear Face

Documented only under cued claustrophobic onset. The change is sudden and complete: pupils dilate, breath shortens to upper-chest, lips part, eyes track rapidly across the boundary surfaces of the enclosure (walls, ceiling). The hands move first to her own throat or sternum — a classic suffocation-anticipation gesture — and then push outward against the nearest surface. The face she shows in this state is, notably, the face of a six-year-old. It is the only context in which her adult composure visibly fails.

---

## IV. VOICE, SPEECH, AND VOCAL TELLS

### Baseline Voice

Contralto, resonant, projected from the diaphragm rather than the throat. Default pace is slow — perhaps 110–120 words per minute against an adult conversational mean of ~150. She does not fill silence. She does not say "um" or "uh"; the absence of disfluency markers is total and worth noting clinically (suggests both high cognitive control and a culturally archaic speech model rooted in the deliberate cadence of oral oratory rather than the elliptical patter of modern American English).

### Accent and Register

The accent is a layered palimpsest: a Kenyan-Egyptian substrate, an overlay of mid-Atlantic English from Xavier-era schooling, and traces of Wakandan court intonation from her marriage years. None dominates; the blend is hers. Vowels are open and rounded; consonants are crisp without being percussive. She does not contract — "I will" rather than "I'll," "cannot" rather than "can't" — except in moments of relaxed intimacy, where she will. The use of contractions is therefore a reliable thermometer of her trust state with the interlocutor.

### Diction Under Stress

Diction *formalizes* under stress, becoming more archaic, more measured, more invocational. The "goddess voice" is real and observable; it is what she defaults to when she needs to regulate herself by regulating her own speech. Under truly severe stress she will slip into one of the three languages of her childhood — Arabic, Swahili, or Amharic — usually a single phrase or oath, almost always under her breath. This is one of the most reliable indices that she has reached her actual operational limit.

### Whisper / Confidential Voice

Drops further in pitch when intimate. With Yukio she has been observed speaking at conversational pitch even in crowded rooms; with lovers she goes very quiet, almost subvocal. The whisper is unhurried.

### Silence

She is unusually comfortable with silence and uses it actively. A long pause from her in conversation is not absence of response; it is response. Subordinates and students learn to wait. The pause length she will hold without breaking it has been observed to exceed thirty seconds in council settings.

---

## V. GROOMING, ADORNMENT, AND SELF-PRESENTATION

### Hair

The white hair is the subject's most recognizable feature and she tends to it with quiet, near-daily ritual. Texture is thick, coarse, naturally tightly coiled when grown out long, which she has worn it for most of her career; the punk mohawk phase (1984–c.1986) was the principal deviation. Care regimen, reconstructed: morning oiling (probably shea or a related African plant butter), evening combing with a wide-tooth instrument, weekly deep conditioning. She does not use heat tools. She has never dyed it — the color is congenital, a mutation marker present from birth.

She handles her own hair in moments of thought. Specific gesture: lifts a single lock from the temple, runs it between thumb and forefinger to the end, releases. Slow, contemplative, often done while reading. This is the most frequently observed hand-to-body self-touch in the record.

In the field, she binds the hair back with a leather thong or simple twist. Loose hair is for solitude and for intimates.

### Skin

Skin care is minimal — water, an oil, sun exposure she does not avoid. No makeup outside of formal Wakandan court appearances and certain Krakoan ceremonies, where she submits to it as a duty. The skin shows almost no aging across her published existence (consistent with X-gene-associated slowed senescence), but she would tend it the same regardless.

### Scent

Personal scent: subtle, plant-based. Rain on warm stone is the closest natural analog. There is no documented perfume use; the smell is partly genuine ambient (she moves through her own atmospheric envelope) and partly the residue of the oils and plant matter she handles in her gardens. Sweat occurs but does not develop strong odor — likely a mutation-adjacent thermoregulatory feature.

### Dress

Civilian dress preference: flowing, layered, in earth and sky palettes — bone, indigo, sand, deep brown, soft white. Fabrics are natural — linen, cotton, silk, leather. She avoids constricting cuts; nothing is tight at the throat or wrists. Sleeveless preferred when context allows. She is barefoot whenever she can be — at home, in gardens, in private councils on Krakoa, in her own quarters on Arakko. Shoes when worn are flat or low-heeled; she has never been observed in a stiletto.

Formal dress (cape, crown, regalia) is donned with ceremonial slowness and is treated as armor. She does not idly adjust her crown or cape in public; once on, they are simply part of her.

The mohawk-leather phase (~1984–1986) is the only documented period of aggressive sartorial reinvention. Black leather, studs, the deliberate carrying of a knife in a visible thigh sheath. The dress in that phase served a psychological function (re-individuation post-depowering) that does not recur; she returned to flowing natural fabrics afterward and has stayed there.

### Adornment

Earrings habitually worn — small, often in matched pairs, often metal. Lifts a hand to touch one occasionally when thinking, in a gesture mirroring the hair-stroke. No nose or other facial piercings. The mohawk phase added a single ear-cuff; she retired it. Bracelets and arm-rings worn ceremonially. No rings on the hands except during her marriage to T'Challa. No timepiece — she reads time from the sun, sky, and her own body.

---

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

### Environment

Sleeps with windows open, skylights uncovered, curtains drawn back. This is non-negotiable; she has refused quarters that could not be made this way and has been observed to drag bedding to balconies or rooftops when no such room could be arranged. On Krakoa, her quarters were grown by Krakoan biology to her specification — open-sided, canopied with living foliage, oriented to the prevailing wind. On Arakko, similar. At the Jean Grey School her room had the largest skylight in the building, by her quiet request.

She will not sleep in a windowless room voluntarily. Forced to (submarine, bunker, sealed safehouse), she sleeps poorly, light, with cued claustrophobic dreams, and wakes in the small hours unable to return.

### Sleep Position

Supine, arms loose at sides or one across the lower abdomen, palms up. She does not curl. She does not bury her face in the pillow. The position is open — the somatic opposite of fetal — and is consistent with the trauma-counter pattern that organizes much of her sleep behavior. With a trusted partner she will sleep on her side facing them but with her own back uncovered toward the room and the door, a sentry's orientation she does not appear conscious of.

### Architecture

Mutant physiology likely reduces total sleep need somewhat; observed nightly window is approximately 5–6 hours. Sleep onset is rapid — within minutes — when conditions are right. She wakes before dawn, almost universally, regardless of bedtime. The pre-dawn rise is one of the most consistent behavioral signatures on the entire record. She uses the first hour after waking for unhurried solitude.

### Dreams

Dream content reported sparingly across canon, but where reported it is sky-imagery, water-imagery, ancestral matrilineal figures, and recurrent intrusions of the buried-alive scenario. The intrusions are most frequent in the days following any actual confinement event. The capacity for lucid management of nightmare appears to have developed across decades — she does not wake screaming; she wakes, breathes, opens a window if one is closed, returns to sleep or rises.

---

## VII. EATING, DRINKING, AND CONSUMPTION

### Diet

Largely plant-based. Heavy on vegetables, grains, fruits, legumes. Modest fish intake in coastal settings. Meat consumed in ceremonial contexts (Wakandan court, certain Krakoan feasts) but not preferred. She grows much of what she eats when conditions allow; the gardens are not decorative.

### Pace and Manner

Eats slowly, in small bites, chewing thoroughly. Sets the utensil down between bites — a habit that signals satiety to the nervous system and that she likely acquired deliberately. Posture at table is the same as standing posture: spine long, shoulders down. Does not lean on her elbows. Does not speak with food in her mouth. The table manners are consistent across all observed contexts from royal banquet to bunk-bed mess hall.

### Quantity

Eats less than her caloric expenditure would predict, and has occasionally been observed to skip meals without apparent distress. The body appears to draw on ambient atmospheric energy in ways not fully understood; mutation-active phases show reduced food requirement. The depowered period showed normal-range intake.

### Drink

Water is the dominant beverage — drunk slowly, often warm rather than cold. Tea daily, frequently a strong dark Kenyan black or an herbal of her own garden. Coffee occasionally, Wakandan or Egyptian preparation, strong and unsweetened. Alcohol: ceremonial only, and minimal — a single glass of wine at a state dinner, a sip of a toast. She does not drink to relax and is one of the most documented near-teetotalers in the X-Men cohort. No record of intoxication; the loss of motor and verbal control would be intolerable to her.

### Stress and Eating

Under stress, intake decreases. She does not stress-eat. She also does not refuse food as protest; she simply forgets to eat. Allies who know her well will bring her tea and small food in a crisis without asking, because she will accept it but not request it.

---

## VIII. STATE-DEPENDENT VARIATIONS

### Calm (Baseline)

All the above. Long spine, soft face, slow breath (~10–12 breaths per minute, nasal, diaphragmatic), low blink rate, hands open, voice unhurried. Ambient weather neutral within several meters of her — a faint cool freshness, no more.

### Mild Stress (council debate, awkward diplomacy, irritation)

Diction formalizes. Contractions vanish from speech. Hand-to-hair or hand-to-earring frequency increases very slightly. The diplomatic smile may appear and persist. Breath does not change visibly. The body holds. Ambient air pressure within the room can shift by a hair — observers with barometric sensitivity have reported a feeling of "weight" entering the space.

### Tactical Stress (combat, command under fire)

The body shifts to a heightened economy. All extraneous movement disappears. Speech becomes terse, declarative, present-tense, often imperative. Eye scan rate increases dramatically. Pulse rises but breath remains controlled, four-count nasal in and out. Hands shift to a ready position — slightly forward of the hips, fingers extended, palms angled. She begins moving in three-dimensional space (up, more often than across). Ambient weather *begins to respond* — wind direction may shift, humidity may drop or climb, ambient light may dim or sharpen. This is not yet weather-working; it is leakage.

### Active Weather-Working

Eyes whiten. The body lifts into the air, often without her appearing to decide to. Arms come up and out, hands open. Hair lifts and stirs in air she is not herself disturbing. Voice deepens further and takes on the genuinely invocational register — the wind-calling speech is in older languages or in vocalizations not strictly verbal. Skin temperature lowers slightly to the touch. She is, in this state, at her most somatically beautiful and her most somatically alien; allies who have not seen it before are typically struck silent.

### Full Affective Break (Rage / Catastrophic Grief)

The rare state. Stillness deepens rather than breaks. Voice may drop to near-whisper. The chin lifts. Eyes go full white. Ambient weather becomes catastrophic on a scale of seconds to minutes — recorded events include the Doom-statue escape hurricane, the Mutant Massacre aftermath storms, certain Arakko skirmishes. The break is total within its window and time-limited; return to baseline begins within minutes of the precipitating cause being neutralized. After the break, the body shows the somatic signs of a parasympathetic rebound: slight tremor in the hands, deep slow breaths, often a slow descent to the ground and a long period of motionless sitting. She will not speak for some time.

### Cued Claustrophobic Onset

The somatic disorganization is severe and unmistakable. Sequence: rapid pupil dilation; upper-chest breathing replacing diaphragmatic; lips part; eyes scan ceiling and walls in saccadic bursts; hand goes first to throat, then to sternum, then to nearest vertical surface; full body weight pushes against that surface; vocalization may include subvocal childhood-language oaths or, in the worst recorded episodes, none — silence and a face flooded with terror. If the enclosure is not relieved within seconds, weather discharge follows. If it can be relieved (a hatch opened, a wall breached), the body re-regulates rapidly but visibly: a long shuddering exhale, hand to face, eyes closed, frequently the need to be in open air immediately afterward, sometimes for hours.

This is the only state in which her composure structurally fails. Every other affective storm she rides; this one rides her.

### Intimacy (Trusted Friendship)

With Yukio specifically, and a small handful of others (Jean, Kitty, occasionally Logan), the body relaxes in registers it does not show elsewhere. She will sit shoulder-to-shoulder. She will lean her head briefly on a friend's shoulder. She will touch a forearm to make a point. She will laugh openly. She will eat sloppily — laughing while chewing, talking around food — in a way she does in no other context. With


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS
## Subject: Ororo Munroe ("Storm")

---

## I. THE TEMPLATE — ORIGINS

Every attachment pattern this subject has produced in fifty years of recorded behavior can be traced, with unusual cleanness, to a four-stage developmental sequence that completed before her twelfth birthday. The cleanness is what makes her unusual: most adult attachment profiles are palimpsests of dozens of caregivers across dozens of years. Hers is composed of four discrete strata, each of which laid down a specific rule that she still operates by.

**Stratum One: The Lost Secure Base (birth to age ~5).** N'Dare and David Munroe are documented in flashback as warm, present, physically affectionate parents in the Cairo apartment on Sharia el-Gomhuriya. The child Ororo had a normal pre-trauma attachment foundation — secure, age-appropriate, with both maternal and paternal poles intact. This matters enormously for prognosis: she had something to remember. Her later capacity to form deep bonds rests on the implicit memory of having once been held without condition. Adults who were never securely attached in infancy do not develop the capacity she demonstrates; adults who were, and then lost it traumatically, can — and she did.

**Stratum Two: The Annihilation (~age 5–6).** The single event: the aircraft, the collapse, hours or days pinned in the dark beside her mother's corpse. The relational lesson encoded — pre-verbal, somatic, indelible — was not "people leave." It was "the person who holds you can be made into a weight on top of you, and you cannot move her, and no one is coming." This is the specific shape of her trauma and it dictates the specific shape of her later relational caution. She does not fear abandonment in the ordinary sense; she fears being held in place by someone who can no longer help her, and being unable to leave.

**Stratum Three: The Exploiter (~age 6–11/12, Cairo).** Amahl Farouk, the Shadow King, took her in as a child thief. He fed her, sheltered her, trained her hands, and — crucially — was the first adult to offer her any structure after her parents' death. He was also a psychic predator who used her. The lesson: *the one who feeds you may be eating you*. This is the precise origin of her warm-formality-at-first-encounter pattern. She gives nothing important early. She watches. She remembers that the man who took her in was a monster, and that she did not see it until she was old enough to see it.

**Stratum Four: The Worshippers (~age 12 to ~young adult, Serengeti/Kilimanjaro).** Reverence, not parenting. She was loved, but as a category — as a rain-bringer, as a goddess. No one looked at her and saw a girl who had been buried alive in Cairo. The lesson: *being adored is not the same as being known*. This installed the lifelong distinction she draws between admirers (of whom she has tens of thousands) and intimates (of whom she has, by my count, roughly seven across five decades). She is courteous to the first category and almost completely closed to it; she is unguarded only with the second.

The composite template, expressible as a single operating rule: **Trust slowly, love completely, expect to grieve alone, and never confuse worship for relationship.**

---

## II. ATTACHMENT CLASSIFICATION

In standard Adult Attachment Interview terms, the subject presents as **earned-secure** with two specific residual features:

1. A **dismissing-leaning coping style under acute distress** — she withdraws upward and outward (to high places, to solitude, to weather) before she reaches for another person. This is not avoidant attachment in the pathological sense; it is the trace of a child who learned that the person beside her could not help and that she had to wait out the dark alone. She has retrofitted this into a positive practice (chosen solitude, meditation, the long flight at altitude) but the underlying somatic move — *away and up, not toward* — is constant.

2. A **selectively unguarded intimacy register** with a very small number of people. With those people the closure drops absolutely. There is no in-between mode. She is either at warm-formality (default with 99% of contacts) or at full transparency (with her seven). She does not have a wide ring of mid-tier confidants. This is unusual for a public figure of her stature and is itself a tell — it suggests that intimacy for her requires a complete release of the watchfulness installed by Farouk, and that the cost of that release is high enough that she does not pay it casually.

The earned-secure classification is supported by the durability of her bonds (Yukio, Forge, T'Challa, Logan, Jean, Kitty all span decades; none have been discarded), the absence of the cyclical idealization-devaluation patterns that mark unresolved attachment, and her demonstrated capacity for *repair* — which is the single best earned-secure marker and which the subject excels at.

---

## III. HOW SHE BONDS

The bonding sequence is highly stereotyped and observable across every documented intimate relationship in her file. There are five phases and they always run in this order.

**Phase 1 — The Long Look.** First contact with anyone she might bond with begins with a period of unhurried observation. She watches how they treat people who cannot benefit them. She watches how they handle their own anger. She watches whether they lie to children. This is not performed scrutiny; it is the ambient state she is in with everyone. The duration is variable — with Yukio it telescoped to days because Yukio's wildness was self-evident and Storm needed to know whether the wildness was cruel (it wasn't); with T'Challa it took months of formal court interaction; with Logan it took years of shared combat before she allowed him into the inner ring.

**Phase 2 — The Test of Equality.** Once she has begun to consider someone, she gives them a small piece of authority over her — defers to their judgment on something modest, accepts their correction without resistance, asks their opinion on a matter she could resolve alone. This is a deliberate experiment: does this person inflate when given power over her, or hold it carefully? Yukio passed by promptly making fun of her. Forge passed by being technically right and gracious about it. Callisto failed initially (used the leverage) and then partially passed years later (returned it). Cyclops, interestingly, has never fully passed — he tends to accept her deference rather than disclaim it, and her relationship with him therefore remained collegial rather than intimate across all eras.

**Phase 3 — The Disclosure of a Wound.** This is the threshold ritual. She will, once she has decided, tell the person something true about her own injury — usually something about the buried-alive event, the claustrophobia, the Shadow King, or her mother. She does not narrate the whole; she gives one image. Forge received the image of the dark. T'Challa received her mother's name. Kitty received the description of the weight. This is the moment the relationship becomes intimate by her definition. She has put a key in the other person's hand. What she watches next is whether they pocket it casually, brandish it, or hold it like something fragile.

**Phase 4 — The Folding-In.** After successful disclosure, she folds the person into her routines. They are invited into her atrium-garden, into the high places where she sleeps with the sky open, into the meditative spaces. Physical proximity in the spaces she has organized for her own regulation is her highest gesture of intimacy — higher, in her economy, than sexual access. Logan was permitted to sit in her loft and not speak. T'Challa was given a key to her private rooftop in Wakanda. Yukio sleeps on her floor when she visits, with the doors open. The folding-in is reciprocal and ongoing; once folded in, a person stays folded in unless they violate the bond catastrophically.

**Phase 5 — The Stewardship Transfer.** The final phase, reached with only a few. She begins to consider the other person's wellbeing as one of the things in her care. This is consequential because her stewardship drive is the strongest force in her psychology; once you are in it, she will make significant operational sacrifices for you without notifying you. Kitty is in this circle. Jean was. T'Challa was for the duration of their marriage and arguably still is. Yukio is. Logan is. Forge, with complications, is. After someone is in the stewardship circle, ending the relationship does not remove them from it — see the Forge separations, see the Wakanda annulment. She continues to tend.

---

## IV. ROMANTIC AND SEXUAL PATTERNING

The subject's romantic record is small, deliberate, and patterned. Three primary partners over fifty years: Forge, T'Challa, and (more ambiguously and intermittently) Logan. Brief flirtations and adjacencies exist (Bishop, Wolverine, others depending on continuity) but the three above are the substantive cases.

**Common features of all three:**
